CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "auth_group_permissions" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "group_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_group" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "permission_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_permission" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "auth_user_groups" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "user_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "group_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_group" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "auth_user_user_permissions" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "user_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "permission_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_permission" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "django_admin_log" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "action_time" datetime NOT NULL, "object_id" text NULL, "object_repr" varchar(200) NOT NULL, "change_message" text NOT NULL, "content_type_id" integer NULL REFERENCES "django_content_type" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "user_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "action_flag" smallint unsigned NOT NULL CHECK ("action_flag" >= 0));

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "homepage_reference" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "refid" varchar(200) NOT NULL UNIQUE, "title" varchar(500) NOT NULL, "journal" varchar(200) NOT NULL, "year" smallint unsigned NOT NULL CHECK ("year" >= 0), "doi" varchar(100) NULL UNIQUE, "date" date NOT NULL, "curator_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "volume" varchar(30) NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "lipids_lipid" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "name" varchar(4) NOT NULL UNIQUE, "lmid" varchar(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE, "com_name" varchar(200) NOT NULL UNIQUE, "search_name" varchar(300) NOT NULL, "iupac_name" varchar(500) NOT NULL, "formula" varchar(30) NOT NULL, "core" varchar(200) NOT NULL, "main_class" varchar(200) NOT NULL, "sub_class" varchar(200) NOT NULL, "l4_class" varchar(200) NOT NULL, "pubchem_cid" varchar(50) NOT NULL, "img" varchar(100) NULL, "date" date NOT NULL, "slug" varchar(50) NOT NULL, "curator_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "sys_name" varchar(200) NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "membranes_membranedoi" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "doi" varchar(50) NOT NULL);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "membranes_membranetopol" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "name" varchar(100) NOT NULL, "temperature" integer unsigned NOT NULL CHECK ("temperature" >= 0), "equilibration" integer unsigned NOT NULL CHECK ("equilibration" >= 0), "mem_file" varchar(100) NULL, "compo_file" varchar(100) NULL, "other_file" varchar(100) NULL, "nb_lipids" integer unsigned NULL CHECK ("nb_lipids" >= 0), "description" text NOT NULL, "date" date NOT NULL, "curator_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "forcefield_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "forcefields_forcefield" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "membrane_id" integer NULL REFERENCES "membranes_membrane" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "software_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "forcefields_software" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "search_name" varchar(100) NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "membranes_membranetopol_doi" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "membranetopol_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "membranes_membranetopol" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "membranedoi_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "membranes_membranedoi" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "properties_analysissoftware" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "software" varchar(50) NOT NULL);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "properties_li_property" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "search_name" varchar(100) NOT NULL, "prop" varchar(3) NOT NULL, "data_file" varchar(100) NULL, "index" integer unsigned NULL CHECK ("index" >= 0), "description" text NOT NULL, "date" date NOT NULL, "curator_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "membranetopol_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "membranes_membranetopol" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "software_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "properties_analysissoftware" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
